    function setIframeHeight(iframe) {
        if (iframe) {
            var iframeWin = iframe.contentWindow || iframe.contentDocument.parentWindow;
            iframe.height = 100;
            if (iframeWin.document.body) {
                iframe.height = iframeWin.document.documentElement.scrollHeight + 50 || iframeWin.document.body.scrollHeight + 50;
            }
        }
    };
    function setIframeHeight1(iframe) {
        if (iframe) {
            var iframeWin = iframe.contentWindow || iframe.contentDocument.parentWindow;
            if (iframeWin.document.body) {
                iframe.height = iframeWin.document.documentElement.scrollHeight || iframeWin.document.body.scrollHeight;
            }
        }
    };

    window.onload = function () {
        setIframeHeight(document.getElementById('mainFrame'));
    };
    window.onresize = function () {
        setIframeHeight1(document.getElementById('mainFrame'));

        window.setInterval("setIframeHeight1(document.getElementById('mainFrame'))", 1000);
    };

</script>

            var str = getQueryString("TT"); //取得本项目开始时间
            str = str.substring(0, 19);
            str = str.replace(/-/g, '/');
            var endDate = new Date(str);
            var end = endDate.getTime();
            window.onload = function countTime()
            {
                //获取当前时间
                var date = new Date();
                var now = date.getTime();

                //时间差
                var leftTime = end - now;

                if (leftTime > 0  )
                {
                    //定义变量 d,h,m,s保存倒计时的时间
                    var d, h, m, s;
                    if (leftTime >= 0) {
                        d = Math.floor(leftTime / 1000 / 60 / 60 / 24).toString();
                        if (d.length <= 1) d = "0" + d;
                        h = Math.floor(leftTime / 1000 / 60 / 60 % 24).toString();
                        if (h.length <= 1) h = "0" + h;
                        m = Math.floor(leftTime / 1000 / 60 % 60).toString();
                        if (m.length <= 1) m = "0" + m;
                        s = Math.floor(leftTime / 1000 % 60).toString();
                        if (s.length <= 1) s = "0" + s;
                    }

                    //递归每秒调用countTime方法，显示动态时间效果
                    document.getElementById("time").innerText = "";
                    if (d == "00") //24小时之内的才显示
                        document.getElementById("time").innerText = h + ":" + m + ":" + s;

                    //else
                        //document.getElementById("time").innerText = d + ":" + h + ":" + m + ":" + s;

                    if (d == "00" && h == "00" && m == "00" && s == "00")  //结束
                    {

                        document.getElementById("time").innerText = "";
                        document.getElementById("btn1").click();
                        //window.location.href("JW_UserDL.aspx");

                    }
                    else setTimeout(countTime, 1000);
                }
            }


            function getQueryString(name) {
                var reg = new RegExp("(^|&)" + name + "=([^&]*)(&|$)");
                var r = window.location.search.substr(1).match(reg);
                if (r != null) {
                    return decodeURIComponent(r[2]);
                }
                return '';
            }

            var str = getQueryString("TT"); //取得本项目开始时间
            str = str.substring(0, 19);
            str = str.replace(/-/g, '/');
            var endDate = new Date(str);
            var end = endDate.getTime();
            window.onload = function countTime()
            {
                //获取当前时间
                var date = new Date();
                var now = date.getTime();

                //时间差
                var leftTime = end - now;

                if (leftTime > 0  )
                {
                    //定义变量 d,h,m,s保存倒计时的时间
                    var d, h, m, s;
                    if (leftTime >= 0) {
                        d = Math.floor(leftTime / 1000 / 60 / 60 / 24).toString();
                        if (d.length <= 1) d = "0" + d;
                        h = Math.floor(leftTime / 1000 / 60 / 60 % 24).toString();
                        if (h.length <= 1) h = "0" + h;
                        m = Math.floor(leftTime / 1000 / 60 % 60).toString();
                        if (m.length <= 1) m = "0" + m;
                        s = Math.floor(leftTime / 1000 % 60).toString();
                        if (s.length <= 1) s = "0" + s;
                    }

                    //递归每秒调用countTime方法，显示动态时间效果
                    document.getElementById("time").innerText = "";
                    if (d == "00") //24小时之内的才显示
                        document.getElementById("time").innerText = h + ":" + m + ":" + s;

                    //else
                        //document.getElementById("time").innerText = d + ":" + h + ":" + m + ":" + s;

                    if (d == "00" && h == "00" && m == "00" && s == "00")  //结束
                    {

                        document.getElementById("time").innerText = "";
                        document.getElementById("btn1").click();
                        //window.location.href("JW_UserDL.aspx");

                    }
                    else setTimeout(countTime, 1000);
                }
            }


            function getQueryString(name) {
                var reg = new RegExp("(^|&)" + name + "=([^&]*)(&|$)");
                var r = window.location.search.substr(1).match(reg);
                if (r != null) {
                    return decodeURIComponent(r[2]);
                }
                return '';
            }

               <td>如果是在录入数据保存过程中，有可能是你的数据有问题，例如日期格式必须是yyyy-MM-dd格式，数字不是半角等；</td>
            </tr>
            <tr>
               <td>4、</td>
               <td>如果你是在导入EXCEL文件时出错，有可能是你的文件的原因，例如文件不是XLS格式，或者文件中了宏病毒等；</td>
            </tr>
            <tr>
               <td>&nbsp;</td>
